    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer1448491796359871778">Eveline Armstrong is fiercely loved and protected by her powerful clan, but outsiders consider her “touched.” Beautiful, fey, with a level, intent gaze, she doesn’t speak. No one, not even her family, knows that she cannot hear. Content with her life of seclusion, Eveline has taught herself to read lips and allows the outside world to view her as daft. But when an arranged</span>
  <span id="freeText1448491796359871778" style="display:none">Eveline Armstrong is fiercely loved and protected by her powerful clan, but outsiders consider her “touched.” Beautiful, fey, with a level, intent gaze, she doesn’t speak. No one, not even her family, knows that she cannot hear. Content with her life of seclusion, Eveline has taught herself to read lips and allows the outside world to view her as daft. But when an arranged marriage into a rival clan makes Graeme Montgomery her husband, Eveline accepts her duty—unprepared for the delights to come. Graeme is a rugged warrior with a voice so deep and powerful that his new bride can hear it, and hands and kisses so tender and skilled that he stirs her deepest passions.<br /> <br />Graeme is intrigued by the mysterious Eveline, whose silent lips are ripe with temptation and whose bright, intelligent eyes can see into his soul. As intimacy deepens, he learns her secret. But when clan rivalries and dark deeds threaten the wife he has only begun to cherish, the Scottish warrior will move heaven and earth to save the woman who has awakened his heart to the beautiful song of a rare and magical love.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1448491796359871778" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1255574016" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1255574016" />
    <a title="Navessa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18104163-navessa"><img alt="Navessa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1444162983p2/18104163.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1255574016?book_show_action=true">Apr 15, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Navessa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Navessa" href="/user/show/18104163-navessa">Navessa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18104163-navessa?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18104163-navessa?shelf=highlanders">highlanders</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1255574016" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9019260612994241139"><b>So. Goddamn. Cheesy.</b><br/><br/>I was tempted to leave the rating for this blank, because uuuuuuuugh. It's me, isn't it? I mean, come on, what's not to love here? Deaf heroine, non-rapey male lead, well-researched historical setting. <br/><br/>PLUS, MEN IN KILTS.<br/><br/>Dat cheese tho...<br/><br/>And to be honest, I wasn't a fan of how females were portrayed, especially in the first 50%. This is a tale of star-crossed lovers, where the king orders a marriage between two rival clans. The female lead is forced to leave her home and fami</span>
  <span id="freeText9019260612994241139" style="display:none"><b>So. Goddamn. Cheesy.</b><br /><br />I was tempted to leave the rating for this blank, because uuuuuuuugh. It's me, isn't it? I mean, come on, what's not to love here? Deaf heroine, non-rapey male lead, well-researched historical setting. <br /><br />PLUS, MEN IN KILTS.<br /><br />Dat cheese tho...<br /><br />And to be honest, I wasn't a fan of how females were portrayed, especially in the first 50%. This is a tale of star-crossed lovers, where the king orders a marriage between two rival clans. The female lead is forced to leave her home and family to marry the enemy. She arrives there, and the men treat her fine, while ALL the women in the clan save one (her new sister in law) are fucking horrible to her. I mean really, really terrible. ALL. OF. THEM. <br /><br />Then, boom, they have a change of heart. It happened so swiftly that it was literally un-believable. Yet the female lead immediately forgives them. Because she's some sort of fucking saint. I did not. Because I am not some sort of fucking saint. I wanted to see them suffer. Alas, they did not. <br /><br /><b><a href="http://www.thealliterates.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thealliterates/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thealliterates" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/the_alliterates/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/thealliterates/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9019260612994241139" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_363275188" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/363275188" />
    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/363275188?book_show_action=true">Jul 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=reviewed-for-netgalley">reviewed-for-netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=reviewed-by-me">reviewed-by-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=first-in-series-trilogy-duet">first-in-series-trilogy-duet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2012-reads">2012-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=books-for-review">books-for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=historical-romance-highlanders">historical-romance-highlanders</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-maya-banks">author-maya-banks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=location-scotland">location-scotland</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-montgomerys-armstrongs">series-montgomerys-armstrongs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer363275188" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer898288620176569467"><br/><i>Never Seduce a Scot</i> is the first book in Maya Banks’ <i>The Montgomerys and the Armstrongs</i> series, and fun, sexy, entertaining tale! From beginning to end, these feuding clans made this a story filled with twists and turns, situations that were both heartbreaking and inspiring, and kept me turning page after page to see what was going to happen next. <blockquote><i>Blurb:</i> Eveline Armstrong is fiercely loved and protected by her powerful clan, but outsiders consider her “touched.” Beautiful, fey, with a level, int</blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText898288620176569467" style="display:none"><br /><i>Never Seduce a Scot</i> is the first book in Maya Banks’ <i>The Montgomerys and the Armstrongs</i> series, and fun, sexy, entertaining tale! From beginning to end, these feuding clans made this a story filled with twists and turns, situations that were both heartbreaking and inspiring, and kept me turning page after page to see what was going to happen next. <blockquote><i>Blurb:</i> Eveline Armstrong is fiercely loved and protected by her powerful clan, but outsiders consider her “touched.” Beautiful, fey, with a level, intent gaze, she doesn’t speak. No one, not even her family, knows that she cannot hear. Content with her life of seclusion, Eveline has taught herself to read lips and allows the outside world to view her as daft. But when an arranged marriage into a rival clan makes Graeme Montgomery her husband, Eveline accepts her duty—unprepared for the delights to come. Graeme is a rugged warrior with a voice so deep and powerful that his new bride can hear it, and hands and kisses so tender and skilled that he stirs her deepest passions.<br /> <br />Graeme is intrigued by the mysterious Eveline, whose silent lips are ripe with temptation and whose bright, intelligent eyes can see into his soul. As intimacy deepens, he learns her secret. But when clan rivalries and dark deeds threaten the wife he has only begun to cherish, the Scottish warrior will move heaven and earth to save the woman who has awakened his heart to the beautiful song of a rare and magical love.</blockquote> Anyone who has read Maya Banks’ contemporaries knows that this woman can write burn up the pages sex scenes, but I wasn’t sure how she’d pull off a non-erotic story. Well, it’s an understatement to say I wasn’t disappointed and, for the record, this is one steamy read.<br /><br />Given the nature of this story I was a tad concerned that the internal dialog would be dry, making the story drag. But I’m happy to say that Ms. Banks’ did a great job of taking inside Eveline’s mind, letting us get to know her and making her thoughts a pleasure to read! At no time did this necessary storytelling bog down the story, and for that I am very grateful!<br /> <br />I can’t often say that I adored the heroine as much as I did the hero but, in this case, I can. Eveline was such a strong, determined young woman who could have justifiably been whiny and bitchy, but she wasn’t. She was feisty, compassionate, loving, forgiving… a truly wonderful lady befitting her role of the Laird’s wife. And speaking of the Laird… lordy, was Graeme ever amazing. He had every right to be angry, bitter, vengeful… but he was none of those things… well, he never directed those things toward Eveline. Honest, understanding, tolerant… the kind of man a woman like Evenline deserves. They were perfectly matched and their <i>happily ever after</i> was hard earned and well deserved.<br /><br />The bottom line: <i>Never Seduce a Scot</i> is a delightful, sexy story. While I would have loved to have heard a more distinctly highlander voice given to the dialog, I truly enjoyed the way this tale was told. I’m very much looking forward to reading the next installment in this series, <i>Highlander Most Wanted.</i><br /><br /><i>My thanks to netgalley.com for providing me with a copy of this eARC in behalf of Ballentine Books, a division of Random House Publishing Group, in exchange for an honest review!</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="898288620176569467" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1327512252" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1327512252" />
    <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy"><img alt="Stacey is Sassy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474185067p2/12062194.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1327512252?book_show_action=true">Jul 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacey is Sassy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacey is Sassy" href="/user/show/12062194-stacey-is-sassy">Stacey is Sassy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/15804294-never-seduce-a-scot">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12062194-stacey-is-sassy?shelf=highlander">highlander</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1327512252" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16314420176376241356"><strong>They thought her daft but she outsmarted them all...</strong><br/><br/>This was a re-read of a favourite historical highland romance. Never Seduce a Scot tells a tale of surprising love between a couple whose families are sworn enemies. The King had demanded that a truce be struck between the feuding clans and stipulated that the Montgomery Laird marry the Armstrong Laird's daughter. Wonderful idea from a king wanting peace but with a bride thought to be daft, there is no happiness to be found for either family.<br/><br/>5 </span>
  <span id="freeText16314420176376241356" style="display:none"><strong>They thought her daft but she outsmarted them all...</strong><br /><br />This was a re-read of a favourite historical highland romance. Never Seduce a Scot tells a tale of surprising love between a couple whose families are sworn enemies. The King had demanded that a truce be struck between the feuding clans and stipulated that the Montgomery Laird marry the Armstrong Laird's daughter. Wonderful idea from a king wanting peace but with a bride thought to be daft, there is no happiness to be found for either family.<br /><br />5 star reads for me are mainly determined by the feelings I get and this one had me feeling heaps. I was devastated for Eveline and the troubles and heartache she faced from her condition. She lived a lonely life with the Armstrong's and decided to not hide behind the daftness when she moved. These changes were not easy and were made harder because of the clan's hatred of her family. There were times I was blubbering like a baby at the hatred and mistreatment she faced. Her determination to be accepted was amazing. She tried to smile through it all, you just can't help but love her.<br /><br />Graeme is the Laird of the Montgomery's and he takes the job very seriously. When he was shackled to a daft woman, he resigned himself to a marriage in name only. His feelings of guilt when he starts to feel lust for his wife were almost humorous. Graeme is a very controlled man who keeps his feelings close to his chest. When his clan treats Eveline badly that control slips and his displeasure is KNOWN. One of my favourite parts to the story was when we see his frustration in wanting everyone to love and accept her like he has.<br /><br />This story has everything I love about historical highland romance. We have a big strong Laird who loves with his whole heart along with a strong and determined heroine. There was no unnecessary angst between the couple, most of the conflict was on the outside. There was a great connection between Graeme and Eveline and enough steamy bits to give me what I like without being OTT. All of the characters play an integral part to keep the story flowing and make you want to know more about them. Even though this was a re-read it was like I was reading it for the first time again. I was sucked in, devoured it and wanted to go back for more.<br /><br />Thanks my lovelies for picking this as our book of the month.<br /><br />This review and more can be found at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://edgyreviews.com/">http://edgyreviews.com/</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16314420176376241356" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_582721140" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/582721140" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/582721140?book_show_action=true">Apr 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/15804294-never-seduce-a-scot">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to • Lisa • by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/6744426-anna">Anna</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer582721140" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10659622763277353796"><b>4.5 AYE LASS STARS.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416522i/822790._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>At the persistence of my gorgeous friend (The beautiful inside and out Anna Champion) and the encouragement of fabulous five star reviews I finally found myself one clicking this popular historical romance and promptly falling happily head over heels. Readers If you want to be swept off your feet then I would suggest that you indulge yourself in a book from this romance genre and specifically if like me you are late to the party and haven't already one clicked this diamond pre</span>
  <span id="freeText10659622763277353796" style="display:none"><b>4.5 AYE LASS STARS.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416522i/822790._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At the persistence of my gorgeous friend (The beautiful inside and out Anna Champion) and the encouragement of fabulous five star reviews I finally found myself one clicking this popular historical romance and promptly falling happily head over heels. Readers If you want to be swept off your feet then I would suggest that you indulge yourself in a book from this romance genre and specifically if like me you are late to the party and haven't already one clicked this diamond prepare for an invasion of the book butterflies and a book that brings home the book enjoyment factor. Welcome to 'Never seduce a scot' and a romance that goes straight for the heart ...<br><br><b>What's it all about</b><br>After a royal decree is made by the king of Scotland a fierce rivalry must come to find peace. The two most powerful clans in the kingdom have always been at war but after the king demands that a marriage is to take place between Laird Armstrong's beloved daughter and Laird Montgomery the feuding Clan's must come together or face war with the king, the union between the two is not received kindly by all involved and so begins the story of Eveline and Graeme. Eveline Armstrong has spent the last two years deceiving her family that an accident on horseback has affected her long term, ridiculed by some as less than normal, Eveline made the choice to protect herself from an less than desirable match of marriage but when the king demands that she forges another union she could not even have imagined what would become of when she meets the powerful but gentlemanly Graeme Montgomery. As this duo start to come to grips with their conflicting emotions regarding loyalty to their blood and lifelong rivalry nothing can come as more than a shock when feelings start to grow. But will this couple make the long rocky Road to happiness when everything says they shouldn't? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416522i/822791._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>This story reminded me of why I love, love. The romance was extraordinary, the story was original and the connection between the couple was heart-in-mouth, I'm- falling-helplessly-in-love beautiful. Of course I was swooning over the delightful characters there is nothing more exciting than two characters falling helplessly in love when everything should stand against them. Eveline stole my heart straight away she was brave, intelligent and has a streak of cheeky that made me smile. Graeme was the most gentlemanly alpha I've ever read about, this hero is wise, loving and ever so delicious, I fell in love with this duo and believed the story the author was portraying about their love. It was a nice break to escape into a book of yesteryear it made my reading experience ever so dreamy, I could not have wanted more from this historical romance and I know this will be the first of many of this genre that I will happily devour.<br><br><b>Why not five?</b><br>I don't want to sound negative here because I genuinely enjoyed this book however there were points in the story that fell somewhat flat for me, where I felt I was just reading instead of involved with what was going on, but there is no mistaking that this is a delightful story and I am fully convinced I will be continuing with the series.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380416522i/822792._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>Do you love romance? yummy hero's? Delightful heroines? Stories that made you swoon? Then this will be a hit for you, and as for those that dismiss historical romance, I suggest you give this one a whirl ... Go grab it readers. Enjoy, kisses.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10659622763277353796" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer4534717101304370957"><a href='http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>

  <span id="freeText4534717101304370957" style="display:none"><a href="http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> || <a href="https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> || <a href="https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> || <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a> || <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a><br><br><br><b>DNF @ 28%</b> <br><br><br><br>*throws book across the room*<br><br><br><br>I gave this author several chances with two of her BDSM series, but both of those were about gross cavemen using BDSM to facilitate their misogynistic 1950s-style-bend-over-and-hand-me-my-martini fantasies from watching too many back to back episodes of <i>Mad Men </i>and <i>Sister Wives </i>on TiVo<i> </i>with a raging hard-on.<br><br><br><br>Surely, I told myself, this sort of antiquated mindset would work better in a costume historical, where if not exactly savory, at least such 'roid rage would at least sort of be easier to swallow (among other things, cough, cough).<br><br><br><br>...NOPE<br><br><br><br>NEVER SEDUCE A SCOT was just as infuriating as the other books by this author that I've read but for different reasons. Those books were bad because they featured some truly awful sex scenes and some really warped views on safe, sane, and consensual kink. This book was infuriating because it takes an utterly Disney approach to history, with two feuding Scottish clans basically sitting back and tolerating one another after a marriage of convenience with only a few petty snips that wouldn't even merit a detention.<br><br><br><br>I was also not very happy with the disability rep. The heroine is deaf, but so shamed by this that she pretends to be mute instead, and somehow managed to instantly pick up lip-reading (no communication issues that would make the plot needlessly complicated). She sustained this injury from falling off a horse, which makes me suspect that she probably regains her hearing at the end of the book, undoubtedly after a bout of cure-all sex with the hero, I'm sure. She also hasn't fully lost her hearing and can still hear deep sounds, and much to her delight, <i>
  <b>the hero's voice is the only voice that she can still hear, despite her deafness</b>
</i>. Oh, how convenient. Let me roll my eyes.<br><br><br><br>As if that weren't enough insult to injury, the heroine is probably one of the most disgustingly precious characters I've encountered in a while, stomping her foot, pouting, winning confidences easily, and just in general being such an annoying little priss that I was shocked nobody professing to hate her (like all of the women in the keep) had made an attempt to hurl her from the ramparts.<br><br><br><br>Methinks that this author is not for me. I think I only paid $1.99 for this book, but even that was too much. It was boring and awful, and now I need to find another Scottish romance for my reading challenge since this one didn't past muster.<br><br><br><br>1 star</span>

<div id="review_521947814" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/521947814" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/521947814?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=highlanders">highlanders</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer521947814" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15061659615364446479">3.5 stars. I'm confused. <b>I'm thoroughly confused.</b> Is this the same author who wrote about a weak-willed woman being <i>repeatedly</i> *cough* utilized by 3 men at the same time in every single possible place there is to utilize a woman? I never would have known that this book came from the same person who wrote the other book if I'd gone into this read blindly. The writing style was <i>completely</i> different.<br/><br/>Okay, I'm not going to lie. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/44488.Colters__Woman__Colters__Legacy___1_' title='Colters' Woman (Colters' Legacy, #1) by Maya Banks' rel='nofollow noopener'>Colters' Woman</a> was not the absolute worst book I've ever read, <i>for what </i></span>
  <span id="freeText15061659615364446479" style="display:none">3.5 stars. I'm confused. <b>I'm thoroughly confused.</b> Is this the same author who wrote about a weak-willed woman being <i>repeatedly</i> *cough* utilized by 3 men at the same time in every single possible place there is to utilize a woman? I never would have known that this book came from the same person who wrote the other book if I'd gone into this read blindly. The writing style was <i>completely</i> different.<br /><br />Okay, I'm not going to lie. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/44488.Colters__Woman__Colters__Legacy___1_" title="Colters' Woman (Colters' Legacy, #1) by Maya Banks" rel="nofollow noopener">Colters' Woman</a> was not the absolute worst book I've ever read, <i>for what it was</i>. That book was fluff erotica - very enticing in parts while completely ridiculous in others (and tiring - how this woman was able to keep up, I'll never know). However, there was nothing about <i>Colters'</i> which made it stand out for me either. The woman was completely downtrodden, the men were interchangeable, and the story was practically nonexistent.<br /><br />Needless to say, my expectations were pretty low for my first highlander read from this author. So you can only imagine my surprise when I found myself enjoying <i>Never Seduce a Scot</i>. <br /><br /><i>Well, who knew I'd end up liking this?</i> Even though the story didn't have as much of the sexy highlander brogue that I love, it was still a touching little read (and not the kind of touching that went on in <i>Colters'</i>). <br /><br />Eveline is a woman who had lost her hearing in an accident involving a horse. Even though Eveline taught herself how to read lips and could understand what people were saying around her, she pretended to be 'daft' and refused to speak in order to avoid being forced into a marriage to a man whom she considered abusive. Instead, she ended up being forced into a 'political' marriage to the head of an enemy clan. <br /><br />Graeme is the man who feels guiltily drawn to his new bride. He doesn't want to believe she is daft, but he does draw the line at trying to make any advances on his wife because he isn't sure where her mental capacity is. He honestly doesn't want to take advantage, even though his instinct is to protect and care for this woman who was dropped into his life and he finds himself attracted to her beauty. I was happily amazed to find that this big, burly, clan leader was really a softie at heart. His attitude was refreshing and different from the general alpha male. Everything about this man showed his strength of character and ability to treat others with respect and kindness. He was a wonderful character.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>To his surprise, she turned just enough to kiss the inside of his hand. It was such a simple thing and yet he felt it all the way to his soul.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />It's not often that you get to read stories in which one of the main characters is disabled in some form and I loved that the author used her real life experiences with her own husband's hearing loss as inspiration for this story. Because Banks drew from her personal knowledge, the story read as authentic and not forced.<br /><br />Overall, this was a beautiful love story and I loved how moving the connection was between Eveline and Graeme. The only fault I could find with the book, which made me knock off half a rating point, is that it ran a little too long. There might have been a benefit from cutting out a few needless scenes. Even so, I'm glad that I gave <i>Never Seduce a Scot</i> a fair chance. I ended up finding a nice little gem in the historical romance genre.<br /><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"I love you, Evangeline," he whispered, though he knew she could not hear him. "Somehow, I'll make you hear me and you'll know that I love you as fiercely as it's possible for a man to love a woman."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15061659615364446479" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_421825381" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/421825381" />
    <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p"><img alt="♡Karlyn P♡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389996373p2/1131400.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/421825381?book_show_action=true">Sep 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♡Karlyn P♡" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p">♡Karlyn P♡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer421825381" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1485858603117599844">Maya Banks is quickly becoming my favorite author of Highlander/Medieval romances. NEVER SEDUCE A SCOT was another winner. It was a sexy, sweet highlander romance between enemy clans. While it was a bit predictable in places, I really didn’t care. The story kept me glued, the characters were endearing, and the romance was swoon worthy. <br/><br/>Forced to marry by the king’s proclamation, Eveline Armstrong and Graeme Montgomery meet just one day before their own wedding. Graeme will respect the king’s wis</span>
  <span id="freeText1485858603117599844" style="display:none">Maya Banks is quickly becoming my favorite author of Highlander/Medieval romances. NEVER SEDUCE A SCOT was another winner. It was a sexy, sweet highlander romance between enemy clans. While it was a bit predictable in places, I really didn’t care. The story kept me glued, the characters were endearing, and the romance was swoon worthy. <br /><br />Forced to marry by the king’s proclamation, Eveline Armstrong and Graeme Montgomery meet just one day before their own wedding. Graeme will respect the king’s wishes, but he has no intention of making Eveline a wife in truth. He will not have the enemy’s daughter be the mother of his children. <br /><br />Shortly after they wed, he realizes the rumors about her being ‘touched’ in the head were a lie. She is deaf, not stupid. She can read lips and communicate just fine. And she has a sweet side that Graeme is very attracted to. <br /><br />His clan has trouble accepting his new bride, now his wife in truth. Someone is also trying to start a war between the Armstrong and Montgomery clans, which puts both of their lives at risk.<br /> <br />There was some great action toward the end, but for most of the book the story is focused on Graeme and Eveline getting to know each other. We learn much about his clan, and meet his brothers (who will have their own stories too)! It was a sweet romance. Graeme was not a dark alpha type hero you normally read about it Highlander/Medieval romances. <br /><br />This was a great start to a new series. It was a bit predictable, but I still recommend it for a fun read. I will definitely read the next, can’t wait. If you like sexy highlander romances, but want a book where the hero isn’t a brooding alpha type, this is a great choice. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1485858603117599844" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12949311096752482740"><b> 3 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>This wasn't quite as good as I thought it'd be. I enjoyed it, but I just thought it was ok. The H was awesome, but I think I've been conditioned to like a different kind of H as he seemed a little too sweet for my liking. I'm sure I'm a minority in that! The ending felt a little lackluster to me too. Many people loved this, so it could just be me 🤷🏻‍♀️<br/><br/><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Eveline and Graeme's story. They are both from enemy clans and the King has orde</span>
  <span id="freeText12949311096752482740" style="display:none"><b> 3 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>This wasn't quite as good as I thought it'd be. I enjoyed it, but I just thought it was ok. The H was awesome, but I think I've been conditioned to like a different kind of H as he seemed a little too sweet for my liking. I'm sure I'm a minority in that! The ending felt a little lackluster to me too. Many people loved this, so it could just be me 🤷🏻‍♀️<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Eveline and Graeme's story. They are both from enemy clans and the King has ordered them to get married to force a blood treaty and cause peace in their area. Eveline had an accident years before and her family believes that she has never fully recovered and is "daft", so they are especially upset about the fact that she is to marry the enemy chieftain and leave to live on their territory. Graeme is sympathetic to Eveline, and they connect instantly regardless of the fact that their families have been enemies for many years. The more time they spend together, the stronger they feel for one another. There is some clan drama, some ex suitor drama, a few sexy times, and some sweet moments...and they get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between focusing mainly on Eveline and Graeme in 3rd person narrative.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. The end felt a little abrupt, but otherwise I never skimmed and I thought it flowed well.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> Kind of. They both felt an instant connection, and it didn't take long for them to feel strongly for each other.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Graeme. I liked him, but he was a little too beta for my preferences. He was so sweet and compassionate towards the h from the start.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 3 stars. Eveline. I though she was ok. I was disappointed in how she didn't trust her family, but I also understood that she was in a bad position.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low, no tissues needed<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Not really <br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Decent. They have some decent tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the storyline.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Ther was an OM that the h was promised to before her accident that comes around and causes some drama. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The h is deaf due to an accident (accident off page), assault/attempted murder (on page), and virgin h.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had ok closure, but I would've liked a farther glimpse into their future. I would still call it a HEA.<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I got it on loan through my public library and Amazon.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be <u>Safe</u> for most safety gang readers<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have the h or H pushing away<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse by mcs<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer441105454" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer14401788362502476638">What a wonderful story!!I absolutely loved this book!!!My first and definetely favorite historical book!!!!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395387ra/761543.gif' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>The story starts with a century of long feud between the Armstrong and Montgomery clans.<br/>The king, having the support of both of these very strong clans fears that his backing will be weakened severely if these 2 clans kill each other off.<br/>Really, it's just a matter of time before they war with each other.<br/>In a last ditch effort to save this from happening the King decides to issue an edict t</span>
  <span id="freeText14401788362502476638" style="display:none">What a wonderful story!!I absolutely loved this book!!!My first and definetely favorite historical book!!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395387ra/761543.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The story starts with a century of long feud between the Armstrong and Montgomery clans.<br>The king, having the support of both of these very strong clans fears that his backing will be weakened severely if these 2 clans kill each other off.<br>Really, it's just a matter of time before they war with each other.<br>In a last ditch effort to save this from happening the King decides to issue an edict that the only daughter of the Armstrong clan must marry the Laird of the Montgomery clan.<br>By uniting the clans in marriage he hopes it will keep them from hurting one another...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395387ra/761544.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>This is met with much anger and hurt on both sides, but what other choice do they have? If they go against the King it will be seen as an act of treason and their clans would be destroyed....<br>For Graeme, not only would that mean tying himself to his fiercest enemy's clan by marriage but it's also known throughout Scotland that the chief's daughter is daft,addled,touched.<br>So it would also mean he couldn't expect a proper wife and therefore his dream of heirs to pass the Montgomery name to is also shattered...<br>It's a crushing blow....<br><br>Graeme<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395387i/761545.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Eveline<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395387i/761546._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved the characters in this book!!<br>Graeme is fair,loyal,caring,protective and open.<br>Eveline is strong,tenacious,sweet,feisty and loving.<br>I found it refreshing to have a heroine that was not "perfect."<br>Their relationship between Graeme and Eveline was incredibility sweet and romantic and I loved the way he stood up for her while she is struggling to gain acceptance into his clan.<br>And while most of the book did revolve around their relationship them getting to know one another and falling in love and they have good chemistry.<br>Their bond is tested as they face challenges,igotry and danger.Their fierce protection of each other is amazing during dire circumstances!!! <br><br><b>Favorite part</b><br><br><br><b>"I appreciate that you seek to protect her Rorie but do not assume that I cannot also give her protection from those who wish her ill.'Tis my duty as her husband and one I do not take lightly.Now sit.The both of you" <br>"My lady,I don't simply care for her.I love her.She is my entire life.Without her,I am nothing.I have nothing".</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395387i/761547.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395387ra/761548.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </span>

    <a title="Karla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3024056-karla"><img alt="Karla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1324910771p2/3024056.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/443080363?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karla" href="/user/show/3024056-karla">Karla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/15804294-never-seduce-a-scot">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Karla by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/2367556-kathleen">Kathleen</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=bevy-of-scrumptious-brothers">bevy-of-scrumptious-brothers</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=kidnapping">kidnapping</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=sweet-romance">sweet-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=scrumptious-scot">scrumptious-scot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=wonderful-caring-man">wonderful-caring-man</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=yummy-men">yummy-men</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=awesome-alpha">awesome-alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3024056-karla?shelf=light-steam-factor">light-steam-factor</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer443080363" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17021293438166397905"><b>4 1/2 Lovely Stars! Great start to this Highlander series!</b> <br/><br/>Beautiful story about two feuding families brought together by through a mandated arranged marriage. Eveline, Graeme and their families are resolved to their fate, not necessarily pleased by the king's order, but they obey to keep peace among the clans. <br/><br/>Eveline was one of the sweetest, bravest heroines I've ever read about, I adored her. Graeme was charming, kind, and even though this union was not what he sought or dreamed about for his</span>
  <span id="freeText17021293438166397905" style="display:none"><b>4 1/2 Lovely Stars! Great start to this Highlander series!</b> <br /><br />Beautiful story about two feuding families brought together by through a mandated arranged marriage. Eveline, Graeme and their families are resolved to their fate, not necessarily pleased by the king's order, but they obey to keep peace among the clans. <br /><br />Eveline was one of the sweetest, bravest heroines I've ever read about, I adored her. Graeme was charming, kind, and even though this union was not what he sought or dreamed about for his marriage or in a wife, he did his best to make Eveline feel at home. What he didn't expect was to fall in love with this beautiful determined girl, that carried the name of his sworn enemy. It was heartbreaking to watch Eveline, who was already afflicted with a disability, overcome the odds, as she tried to win acceptance of Graeme's clan. They humiliate, berate and try to break her, but her iron will and love for Graeme give her the strength she needs to forge ahead. Graeme initially feels pity for her, but her sweet personality, beauty, and sheer tenacity to become an accepted member of the clan, has him thinking that instead of being cursed, he's been blessed. <br /><br />Rorie, Graeme's sister was a delight, and her friendship with Eveline was quick to form, as was her protective nature. Bowen and Teague, Graeme's brothers, angry that Eveline has taken the family name, eventually soften to this woman, who puts herself in harm's way to protect their brother. <br /><br />The ending was somewhat abrupt and I was disappointed that there was no epilogue, but I'm hoping future books in the series will involve both the Armstrong's and the Montgomery's. I enjoy when books feature a couple, but center around the family, giving us a chance to follow the lives of the couples that came before. <br /><br />There are some heated love scenes, but they are few. However, what I enjoyed the most in this book, were the moments were Graeme and Eveline connected through their hearts, and they both realize that the heritage you're born into, doesn't define you as a person. It was really lovely! </span>
  <a data-text-id="17021293438166397905" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1260786653" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1260786653" />
    <a title="Carmen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25353295-carmen"><img alt="Carmen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1412617445p2/25353295.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1260786653?book_show_action=true">Apr 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmen" href="/user/show/25353295-carmen">Carmen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Romance fans</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Carmen by: </span>
      Navessa
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=traditionally-published">traditionally-published</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=she-says">she-says</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=published2012">published2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=american-author">american-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25353295-carmen?shelf=five-romance-stars">five-romance-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1260786653" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4453300506640207009"><i>He liked kissing. Many a man didn't have much patience for it. His men jested about kissing being a waste of time and was only for wooing the unwilling lasses. But if a lass was willing, they'd much rather move to the more rudimentary elements of coupling.<br/><br/>But to Graeme, kissing was almost as intimate as the act of lovemaking itself. It wasn't something to be hurried or to be offered as a token to woo a reluctant lass. It was an expression of regard.</i><br/><br/>Welp, there you have it. *Carmen slams the book</span>
  <span id="freeText4453300506640207009" style="display:none"><i>He liked kissing. Many a man didn't have much patience for it. His men jested about kissing being a waste of time and was only for wooing the unwilling lasses. But if a lass was willing, they'd much rather move to the more rudimentary elements of coupling.<br /><br />But to Graeme, kissing was almost as intimate as the act of lovemaking itself. It wasn't something to be hurried or to be offered as a token to woo a reluctant lass. It was an expression of regard.</i><br /><br />Welp, there you have it. *Carmen slams the book shut.* Now you know why this is getting 5 romance stars from me. Okay, bye.<br />...<br /><br /><br />Oh, you're still here? You want more details about the book? A hero who loves kissing isn't enough for you? Okay.<br /><br />This is an AMAZING romance book that is going to make your heart explode inside your chest. For tons of reasons: cuteness, sweetness, betrayal, shock, outrage, and romance. Yay!<br /><br />The Armstrongs and the Montgomerys hate each other. Their clans have been feuding for generations. So the king orders a marriage to unite the two clans.<br /><br />Eveline Armstrong is touched. Daft. Not right in the head. Her clan is outraged at the thought of her being forced into a marriage with the hated laird Graeme Montgomery. Anyone can see that she is unfit to carry out her wifely duties. Why, she hasn't spoken a single word in three years, not since "the accident."<br /><br />Graeme is not pleased with the arrangement, either. Getting married to a woman who is afflicted means that he will be unable to consummate the marriage and unable to have any heirs. And when he finds himself very attracted to the tiny blonde lass, he is ashamed. Only a slime would think lustful thoughts about a dimwit. And Eveline is most certainly addled... Isn't she?<br /><br />Having faked mental problems for three years, Eveline is tired of pretending that she's touched. In fact, nothing is wrong with her brain at all. She's simply deaf. But in a desperate move to avoid marriage to a wife-beating rapist piece of shit, she used her deafness as a tool to fake intellectual disability. Now, forced by marriage into a clan who hates her family, can she confess the truth and find an ally in her kind and patient husband?<br />...<br /><br />This book is so cute and delicious and it also will make your heart explode with feelings. o.O <br /><br />GRAEME: Sweet, kind, patient, loves kissing (!!!!!). He is so honorable. Sometimes historical heroes can be forceful, possessive, and a bit brutal, so I'm happy to report that Graeme is a complete mensch. Your heart will be melting from the cuteness. He acts so correct, it is so attractive, OMG. Patient men who love kissing are the best in life. O.O I was excited. He's so good with consent. He has a really deep voice and Eveline loves it because she can feel the vibrations from his voice. I'm with you, girl. I could listen to Vin Diesel or Michael Clarke Duncan or Michael Dorn or James Earl Jones or Ving Rhames read me the phone book and it would be exciting. ;) For serious. What else? Oh yeah. As something VERY RARE in a historical romance, Graeme is NOT a mujeriego. NOT a man who has slept with 500 women. He's actually just slept with about 4 or 5. Wow. That is so amazing for this genre you have no idea. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[And when he goes down on Eveline, it's his first time doing that! OMG so sweet. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />EVELINE: Sweet, kind, good-hearted, earnest, hard-working, sincere, smart, and brave. My heart was being torn out every time someone was mean to her because she was deaf or because they thought she was daft. She was always trying to do the right thing and she was so brave. Aw!<br /><br />There's bad guys and betrayal and some bad stuff happens (but no rape, thank you, Banks). This book will really put you through the wringer.<br /><br />I loved every minute of this book.<br /><br />I highly recommend this if you like historical romance, and/or specifically Highlander romance.<br /><br />3 REAL STARS, 5 ROMANCE STARS - Highest romance recommendation!!!<br /><br />P.S. Why is this available in Portuguese and NOT Spanish!?!!?!?!? Grrrrrrrrrrrrrrrr</span>
  <a data-text-id="4453300506640207009" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13055779882606951816">Ugh, just some evidence of my tiny, hard, shriveled heart.<br/><br/>I had some issues with this book, and none of them were necessarily the issues you'd expect from this type of set up.<br/><br/><i> Everything was just so perfect </i><br/>After decades long feud (or more) you come to realize these fighting clans are just made up of the best people. except for the mean girls in the Montgomery clan. Without the mean girls, there'd be no conflict. NONE. Absolutely none. Because the hero is a perfect patient man who says all the r</span>
  <span id="freeText13055779882606951816" style="display:none">Ugh, just some evidence of my tiny, hard, shriveled heart.<br /><br />I had some issues with this book, and none of them were necessarily the issues you'd expect from this type of set up.<br /><br /><i> Everything was just so perfect </i><br />After decades long feud (or more) you come to realize these fighting clans are just made up of the best people. except for the mean girls in the Montgomery clan. Without the mean girls, there'd be no conflict. NONE. Absolutely none. Because the hero is a perfect patient man who says all the right things, repeatedly and is astounded by just how sweet and beautiful the heroine is. And she's astounded that she can hear his vocalizations and just how sweet, patient, and loyal he is. It's just so happy. And they are just so perfect. And just so beautiful. <br /><br />It was <i> SO repetitive </i> between discussions on their beauty, the conflict between the clans, the fact that Eveline tried so hard and Graeme did too, and then that we'd repeat that within the same page in just a different order I feel like the author missed putting any depth or content and just went straight for word count (I could handle this better in audio cause I could kind of space here and there)<br /><br />It was <i> beyond sentimental. </i> Between the repetition and the sentimentality, I wish I could show you a video of how many times I scoffed. Graeme declares his love to Eveline's dad. Then he repeats it to her mom. Almost the exact same phrasing. And it was, like, so sticky. <br /><br />Complicated family drama just brushed aside in favor of this beautiful beautiful love. <br /><br />I was so disappointed for what could have been. Maybe just a tiny bit more reluctance between characters and their families. Maybe not the outrageous mean girls from the Montgomery clan as a method for conflict &amp; the ex-fiance as the final culmination. Plot devices, all. At first, I couldn't believe this was the same author that I weirdly stumbled across that wrote about the woman savior for the Colter Brothers (and yak, don't get me started with that one). Turns out, this is about another woman savior. Everyone just loves her so damn much that nothing else, Nothing Else, matters.<br /><br />It was an easy read. The beginning was really promising. Then it went rapidly to pot.</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4639765-kristin?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer176877466756984751">Eveline has thought to be daft since her spill on a horse years ago. So when the king forms a marriage between two enemy clans regarding Eveline's hand in marriage, her family is outraged. However, to refuse the marriage would be defying the king, but, they do not let her go to their enemies hands lightly and are quick to inform Graeme of Eveline's condition. When she happens upon Graeme and her father speaking, she is instantly taken with him. He is the first person she has ever been able to he</span>
  <span id="freeText176877466756984751" style="display:none">Eveline has thought to be daft since her spill on a horse years ago. So when the king forms a marriage between two enemy clans regarding Eveline's hand in marriage, her family is outraged. However, to refuse the marriage would be defying the king, but, they do not let her go to their enemies hands lightly and are quick to inform Graeme of Eveline's condition. When she happens upon Graeme and her father speaking, she is instantly taken with him. He is the first person she has ever been able to hear. Granted, she can't make out words but she can feel the vibration from his deep timber voice and the fact that that is the first voice she's noticed excites her.<br /><br />Graeme is not too thrilled with this arranged marriage but like the Armstrongs, there is naught he can do about it without gaining the wrath of the king. So he goes along onto enemy land to marry a daft girl. A girl who will most assuredly, due to her condition, never produce an heir, thus ending his line. What he wasn't expecting was a beautiful woman who not only seems taken with him but shows great intellect and awareness as well. He is instantly protective of her and when problems arise back on Montgomery land with his clan not accepting her, he is quick to squash the problem and make an example of those whom are harassing her.<br /><br />This was a great historical romance. I admit that this is the first Maya Banks novel that I have read and I can honestly say that it won't be my last. In fact, I look forward to more from this series. Banks has a great way of telling a story and painting the picture of the grassy green hills of Scotland. I instantly fell in love with the characters and look forward to catching up with them in the next novel. The romance between Eveline and Graeme didn't by any means feel rushed since for a good portion of the book, Graeme thinks her daft and tries to respect her as an innocent woman. I even enjoyed the secondary characters and am quite pleased to find out that this is part of a series. <br /><br /><b>Favorite part...</b><br />Once arriving on Montgomery land after the marriage Eveline is taking to her chamber. Note the "her" and not the "their" chamber. She is not pleased at all that unlike a normal marriage, her husband has placed her in a separate room to his own. So she sets out to rectify this immediately and is caught by Graeme's sister Rorie when she's trying, unsuccessfully I might add, to move her trunks to which ever room might be his. So she asks Rorie to help her not only find Graeme's room but to assist her in moving all of her belongings there.<br /><br />"Rorie burst out laughing. Her sister-in-law wasn't happy over her accommodations and she wanted to move into Graeme's chamber. She should be loyal and sternly inform her brother's new bride that is Graeme had wanted her in his chamber he would have put her there. But the devil on her shoulder told her it could be quite fun to aid Eveline in her endeavor and give Graeme a shock when he retired later."</span>

<div id="review_349680970" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/349680970" />
    <a title="Kathleen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2367556-kathleen"><img alt="Kathleen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451733481p2/2367556.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/349680970?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kathleen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kathleen" href="/user/show/2367556-kathleen">Kathleen</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer349680970" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15209637668133103722">Story rating 5 BIG STARS<br/>Character Rating 5 BIG STARS<br/>Romance Rating 5 BIG STARS<br/>Heat Level 4 out of 5 stars<br/>Overall Rating, priceless, LOL!<br/><br/>Can you tell how much I LOVED this book? Just in case you have not figured out how much, I must say that this book was absolutely AMAZING!<br/><br/>This book grabbed me early on and had me loving every moment. The heroine, Eveline was such a special character. She went into a marriage with her clans most hated enemy and by the end she brought them to her knees with her be</span>
  <span id="freeText15209637668133103722" style="display:none">Story rating 5 BIG STARS<br />Character Rating 5 BIG STARS<br />Romance Rating 5 BIG STARS<br />Heat Level 4 out of 5 stars<br />Overall Rating, priceless, LOL!<br /><br />Can you tell how much I LOVED this book? Just in case you have not figured out how much, I must say that this book was absolutely AMAZING!<br /><br />This book grabbed me early on and had me loving every moment. The heroine, Eveline was such a special character. She went into a marriage with her clans most hated enemy and by the end she brought them to her knees with her beautiful smile and her kind forgiving and gentle heart. Don't think because of that she was wimpy, NO WAY. Eveline was very smart, brave and courageous. Time and time again she did what she thought would help her ease her way into the enemy clan, never once complaining. It was not an easy task and she had many of clan members do offal things to her. <br /><br />The hero, Grarme was also a fantastic hero. I loved watching this fierce warrior fall for Eveline even though she came from the enemy's clan. I loved that we have a hero who had not slept around with every lass. When he finally decided that Eveline was ready to consummate the marriage, he did so very gentle and put her every pleasure above his first. Let me tell you that the love scenes were really written well.<br /> <br />This book brought out many emotions for me. I felt, sadness, joy, anger and of course love. I sighed, smiled, cried and got the chill bumps through out this book.<br /><br />By the end of the book, you got to see just how fiercely these two cared and loved each other. I really could feel the love leaping off of the pages.<br /><br />There are plenty of secondary characters in this book also. Graeme has two brothers and a sister. Eveline has 2 brother also. I wonder who the Hero or Heroine will be in the next book, Highlander Most Wanted. I tell you February 26, 2013 can't come fast enough for me. I'm going to go absolutely crazy waiting on this next installment.<br /><br />After saying all that I just have to say that YES, I would HIGHLY recommend to any and all of my book friends out there who love a fantastic Scottish romance to read this one. I can say without a doubt that you will really like this one, if not LOVE it as I have :-)<br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="15209637668133103722" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2811244267" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2811244267" />
    <a title="Somia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/88350974-somia"><img alt="Somia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568928901p2/88350974.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2811244267?book_show_action=true">May 06, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Somia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Somia" href="/user/show/88350974-somia">Somia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/88350974-somia?shelf=highlander-hotness">highlander-hotness</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/88350974-somia?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2811244267" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11351283099888259654"><b> 4.5 Exuberant Stars </b><br/><br/>This book was a freaking fabulous morsel of highlander magic, the tone of the book is fairly gentle in the first half of the book, but it really, really works, and I’ve ended up devouring the book, thank goodness that due to the bank holiday Monday, work was so quiet, allowing me to get lost in Graeme and Eveline’s tale. <br/><br/>The king in an attempt to put to rest the conflict and hate between two of his greatest allies, decides that a marriage between the clans is the best way to</span>
  <span id="freeText11351283099888259654" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 Exuberant Stars </b><br /><br />This book was a freaking fabulous morsel of highlander magic, the tone of the book is fairly gentle in the first half of the book, but it really, really works, and I’ve ended up devouring the book, thank goodness that due to the bank holiday Monday, work was so quiet, allowing me to get lost in Graeme and Eveline’s tale. <br /><br />The king in an attempt to put to rest the conflict and hate between two of his greatest allies, decides that a marriage between the clans is the best way to go, and the sacrificial lambs are Laird Graeme Montgomery and the only cherished daughter of Laird Armstrong – Eveline.<br /><br />Eveline, a few years ago suffered a fall from her horse, and since then is considered by many to have become ‘daft’ and feebleminded, she is happy to let them think so as it has allowed her to escape a horrid fate, and the fierceness of her father, mother and brothers mean none in her clan will be cruel to her. When she learns about the arranged marriage the king has ordered, something her family despise, she is ready to do her duty, but when she first meets Graeme, she is given an unexpected but welcomed surprise – one which gives her hope for the marriage and new life she is to have. Graeme for his part finds himself fascinated by the beauty that is to be his wife, but believing the rumours about her being ‘touched’, treats her gently, expecting nothing but a marriage in name only.<br /><br />Watching Eveline slowly come out of her shell, her moments of fierceness, and the tenderness between her and Graeme had me entranced. Seriously Graeme rocks in this, the fact he is steadfast in his support of Eveline, fabulously protective and he doesn’t hesitate to show her affection and support in front of his initially highly bitter clan was lovely to see. He also never tries to change her, but takes her exactly as she is, never seeing her as less. <br /><br />There were moments where I wanted to dump some ice-cold water on the women in Graeme’s clan, they made things so hard for Eveline, but she didn’t let them crush her. I grinned with delight when Graeme <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[skewered Ian, the reptile deserved much worse, but I do wish, I had gotten to see Ian’s father be confronted and then get just what he deserved, although I’m thinking it’s possible this may be shown in the next book?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Triggers: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Bullying, violence - Evelin is beaten/punched in the face.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I’m glad I purchased this, it’s staying in my re-read pile, and rather than appease my need for some highlander magic, it has me wanting more.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11351283099888259654" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1827876863?book_show_action=true">Jun 23, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review">Mindy Lou&#39;s Book Review</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/15804294-never-seduce-a-scot">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44132489-mindy-lou-s-book-review?shelf=2019">2019</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1827876863" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7711018036704613333">This has one of the best heroes. He’s protective, caring and didn’t allow hatred to affect his treatment of the heroine, even though she comes from his enemy clan. The heroine was also one of the sweetest. She did not judge and worked desperately to gain favor of her new clan despite her challenges. It’s a soft love story in the middle of two hardened clans hatred.</span>

          </span>
        </div>
